<rating>5<//rating>< text>
I completed both the basic and advanced seminars at Oaksterdam University (OU) on Jan. 30 - Feb. 2, 2016. Doors opened at 9:30 a.m. and class began at 10. The staff at OU are friendly and provide exceptional customer service. One of the staffers, Amanda, manages the seminars with genuine enthusiasm and facilitates a welcoming atmosphere. Doctors, lawyers, and entrepreneurs presented subjects including Politics & History, Criminal & IP Law, Clinical Research, Horticulture, and Advocacy. We even went on a field trip to a local dispensary. I was thoroughly impressed by the professionalism and camaraderie exemplified by my fellow classmates, many of which possessed years of experience and/or three letters at the end of their names. Our networking during the seminars will provide us with future business opportunities.</text>

It was my daughters first visit to this office. It is very kid friendly. She imidiately liked the environment because they were playing a Disney movie and the staff greeted both of us very well. My daughter has anxiety when going to the docor or dentist, She cries even before they do anything to her. Kind of pricey but it is cleaned daily and they run ceiling fans and AC when needed so I stopped going to the sweat shop laundromats. Most employees are friendly and helpful (there's always one or two in every bunch that aren't) the TV's usually have something decently entertaining on if you like to watch it.
They do have dryer specials what I don't like is people come out if the bush that have not washed their clothes there with 7-10 loads right as my laundry is just about to come out of the washer and they take up 7-10 dryers to take advantage of the dryer special. That is not right or fair to loyal customers that do both wash and dry there. I am a twice a week customer that does not even try to come on those days because of the rude dryer hog people that get away with doing that. I just go elsewhere if I need to do my laundry on their dryer special days.This is why I'm rating 4* I was thinking of giving 3* because it pisses me off.< /text>

< review>
Nice neighborhood park with access to the Laguna Creek Trail. Lots of wildlife visible on the trail, particularly during the cooler weather: Snowy Egrets, Great Blue Herons, ducks (including the beautiful Wood Duck)-- even beavers.
Nice Fall color in the park and along the trail. Some fairly large Western Redbud along the trail towards Waterman Rd. Should be spectacular in the Spring.
There's a kiddie playground, a couple of largish playing fields, a couple of baseball diamonds and decent restrooms.</review>
